  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_b1ce8512-f91e-4e83-92b4-f1cc0f1e6c65'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

  <i>Librarian’s note: This is a previously-published edition of<br />paperback <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/40195266-chill-factor" rel="nofollow noopener">ISBN: 9780743466776</a>.</i>
</b><br /><br />Cleary, North Carolina, is a sleepy mountain town—the kind of place where criminal activity is usually limited to parking violations. Not so, lately. Four women have disappeared from Cleary over the past two years. And there’s always a blue ribbon left near the spot where each of the women was last seen. There are no bodies, no other clues, and no suspicion as to who their abductor might be. And now, another woman has disappeared without a trace. <br /><br />It is to this backdrop that Lilly Martin returns to close the sale of her mountain cabin, marking the end of her turbulent eight-year marriage to Dutch Burton, Cleary’s chief of police. Dutch’s reluctance to let her go isn’t Lilly’s only obstacle. As she’s trying to outrun a snowstorm, her car skids on the icy road and strikes a man who emerges from the woods on foot. She recognizes the injured man as Ben Tierney, whom she’d met the previous summer. They’re forced to wait out the storm in the cabin, but as the hours of their confinement mount, Lilly begins to wonder if the greatest danger to her safety isn’t the blizzard outside, but the mysterious man right beside her. <br /><br />Is Ben Tierney the feared abductor? Or is he who he claims to be...her rescuer from harm and from the tragedy that haunts her?</span>
  <a data-text-id="16385472374360910503" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">If you finished the book you will see it all come together. Sandra Brown's books always have great points and are easy reads. All of the characters ar<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">If you finished the book you will see it all come together. Sandra Brown's books always have great points and are easy reads. All of the characters are well built, once again if you don't have the attention span to read this book move on. I loved this book, I felt that the characters were will built and were described what role they played. But look out! All kinds of twists and turns throughout the story!<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

<div id="review_1876804520" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1876804520" />
    <a title="A." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22324639-a"><img alt="A." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1601824977p2/22324639.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1876804520?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="A." class="user" itemprop="url" name="A." href="/user/show/22324639-a">A.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=_romantic-suspense">_romantic-suspense</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=out-in-the-cold">out-in-the-cold</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=small-town-setting">small-town-setting</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=cabin-or-vacation-home">cabin-or-vacation-home</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=pov-3rd-person">pov-3rd-person</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=pov-multiple">pov-multiple</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=loved-the-writing">loved-the-writing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=loved-it">loved-it</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1876804520" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9853558704254682274"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/>Another great novel by Sandra Brown.<br/><br/>This book combines two elements that I love: trapped-in-a-blizzard romance and a small town mystery.<br/><br/>Love, love cabin romances. <br/><br/><blockquote>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494009658ra/22675772.gif' height='400"/' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/><br/>There’s something magical about them. On the one hand, they give me that cozy feeling of being indoors cuddled under the duvet while it snows outside. On the other hand, I love the tension and the slow build-up of the romantic relationship in a confined space (without technology, ow/om drama, manwhoring habits and other cl</span>
  <span id="freeText9853558704254682274" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br><br>Another great novel by Sandra Brown.<br><br>This book combines two elements that I love: trapped-in-a-blizzard romance and a small town mystery.<br><br>Love, love cabin romances. <br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494009658ra/22675772.gif" height='400"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>There’s something magical about them. On the one hand, they give me that cozy feeling of being indoors cuddled under the duvet while it snows outside. On the other hand, I love the tension and the slow build-up of the romantic relationship in a confined space (without technology, ow/om drama, manwhoring habits and other clichéd stuff). <br><br>Although, there is nothing <i>cozy</i> or <i>warm</i> about <i>this</i> cabin romance.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494014954ra/22676176.gif" width='400"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Small towns are perfect settings for thrillers.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494013900ra/22676069.gif" width='400"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Who doesn't like small town mysteries with its variety of quirky, zany characters and their dirty little secrets, illicit love affairs and town gossips that live in everyone else's business?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494020246ra/22676574.gif" width='400"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is definitely a page-turner. It's full of intrigue and it makes you questioning everything and everybody. Sandra Brown once again proved herself as a talented, page turning author.<br><br>My only complaint is the romantic aspect of the story. The book is more focused on suspense than romance and I was okay with that. However, the romantic side of the story was kind of weak. I never connected with the main characters. In fact, I liked the side characters better and enjoyed their stories more than the main characters and their story.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510504825i/24426022._SX540_.jpg" width='400"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="9853558704254682274" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

Eventhough I read the book a while back, I couldn't really remember the bad guy! LOL.<br><br>***********************************************************<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> Four women have disappeared from Cleary over the past two years. And there's always a blue ribbon left near the spot where each of the women was last seen. There are no bodies, no other clues, and no suspicion as to who their abductor might be. And now, another woman has disappeared without a trace. Lilly Martin, a successful magazine editor is trapped in her remote cabin with a man believed to be a serial killer. Is Ben Tierney the feared abductor? Or is he who he claims to be...her rescuer from harm and from the tragedy that haunts her?</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411899833i/11297262.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Really liked this one. Had me on the edge of my seat! I was guessing and second guessing everybody.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>There was little to look at so, eventually they looked at each other</b>

I didn’t lose interest once in the book. My imagination was running wild, wondering what the outcome would be.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411899833i/11297263._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>

  <b>”I think the guy knows that women swoon over that rugged outdoorsy type.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>It had a mixture of small town characters. Some were likeable. Some were not.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411899833i/11297259._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>There was the sheriff, who thought he could do what he wanted. <br>The High School coach who was a bully.<br><br><blockquote>

<div id="review_1067089843" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1067089843" />
    <a title="♥Sharon♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12125670-sharon"><img alt="♥Sharon♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417537732p2/12125670.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1067089843?book_show_action=true">Sep 29, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Sharon♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Sharon♥" href="/user/show/12125670-sharon">♥Sharon♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6382168-chill-factor">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1067089843" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11808205931937999528">4.5 I was so confused stars....<br/><br/>Sandra Browns writing never fails to lure me into the story. With equal doses of suspense and mystery she also has the ability to weave in a certain level of sex appeal in way that creates anticipation and when the moments happen….<br/><br/><a href='http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/chillfactor_zps78605c38.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414891532i/11701919.jpg' alt=' photo chillfactor_zps78605c38.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Let me start by saying this one drove me a little batty. It was fantastic of course but for the first 60% or so my thoughts were spinning in so many different directions that I my little brain was about to explode. <br/><br/><b>Where to begin with</b></span>
  <span id="freeText11808205931937999528" style="display:none">4.5 I was so confused stars....<br><br>Sandra Browns writing never fails to lure me into the story. With equal doses of suspense and mystery she also has the ability to weave in a certain level of sex appeal in way that creates anticipation and when the moments happen….<br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/chillfactor_zps78605c38.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414891532i/11701919.jpg" alt=" photo chillfactor_zps78605c38.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Let me start by saying this one drove me a little batty. It was fantastic of course but for the first 60% or so my thoughts were spinning in so many different directions that I my little brain was about to explode. <br><br><b>Where to begin with this one?</b><br><br>The setting for Chill Factor is a little town called Cleary. It’s that kind of town where everyone knows everyone else’s business. Things are a bit unsettled in Cleary because 5 women have gone missing with no suspect at hand and the only apparent common connection is a blue ribbon found at each location the woman were last seen.<br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/335fef0d-b42f-4842-89b7-f3d461d33ab7_zps07d49ab8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414891532i/11701920.jpg" alt=" photo 335fef0d-b42f-4842-89b7-f3d461d33ab7_zps07d49ab8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Though a threatening storm is approaching <b>Lilly Martin</b> and her ex-husband <b>Dutch Burton</b> head to their winter cabin to remove all their belonging since there will be new owners moving in soon. Their time spent together is tense if nothing else. Things have happened within their lives that has left their relationship strained and broken. Lilly is ready to move on but Dutch, well he hates the thought of not having Lilly in his life.<br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/08d8c296-0c2f-4f3e-9dbe-8c362ce5c9d3_zpsb2fd80ba.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414891532i/11701921.jpg" alt=" photo 08d8c296-0c2f-4f3e-9dbe-8c362ce5c9d3_zpsb2fd80ba.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>As they leave separately to head back down the mountain, things are about to change for both of them. While Dutch makes his way down the mountain through the storm, Lilly isn’t so lucky. Without warning she loses control of her car never expecting to hit a man who is out in the storm. With no other choice they return to her cabin for safety.<br><br>What is surprising to Lilly is she knows this man. It is <b>Ben Tierney.</b> Though their meeting was back in the summer, it was a meeting that neither has forgotten. They had an undeniable attraction then and now that they are confined together who knows what will happen.<br><br>Tierney isn’t a local though. His visits to town have been because of the column he writes for a outdoorsmen magazine. Or so it appears. When distressing information surfaces, and Lilly doesn’t make it down the mountain, the already present tension in town heightens.<br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/7a6bede0e49b3cd90832b8eeb92719eb_zps8c9e913f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414891532i/11701922._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 7a6bede0e49b3cd90832b8eeb92719eb_zps8c9e913f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Felling trapped Lilly doesn’t know what or who to believe. And because neither Ben or herself has a connection with anyone from town they are left with only their thoughts and desire to get off the mountain.<br><br><b>And then it happens.</b><br><br>In true SB form, the last 30% of the book kicked ass!!! With my heading spinning like crazy trying to figure out the connections, trying to get my answers to all my “what the hell moments”, shit starts to happen. From seeing Dutch in true form, to the locals; William Ritt, Marilee Ritt, Wes Hamer and Scott Hamer, I found myself picking my jaw off the floor more than once. I cannot even begin to tell you what goes on. <br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/8418ccc75c55cfece1fbc4555b2a5096_zps895d5d4d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414891532i/11701924._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 8418ccc75c55cfece1fbc4555b2a5096_zps895d5d4d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tierney and Lilly are surviving by a thread. Both are on edge for their own reasons, Lilly’s are apparent but Tierney’s are more of a mystery. With only a fireplace as their source of warmth, human nature and desire takes over.<br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/6a904694-b017-4117-a79c-daafc1de93cd_zpsa3aa74af.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414891532i/11701923.jpg" alt=" photo 6a904694-b017-4117-a79c-daafc1de93cd_zpsa3aa74af.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Neither Lilly nor Tierney were prepared for what was happens between them. With doubt, fear and desperation taking over Lilly’s thoughts, Tierney finds himself saying and doing things he feels he has no other choice with. <br><br>There was no stone unturned in this one. I ended up loving it like all her other books I have recently read. I must say that this one had my favorite epilogue. ❤<br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/d5e7aabf-69c8-4050-88f1-fccbe705f86e_zps069e3c7b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414892252i/11701962.jpg" alt=" photo d5e7aabf-69c8-4050-88f1-fccbe705f86e_zps069e3c7b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="11808205931937999528" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText6283274207133166682" style="display:none">Seems I have broken my audio drought, as wholeheartedly the two main characters with very cool names - Lilly and Tierney - survived their blizzard and crazy circumstances. <br /><br />This romantic thriller (what a great combo this is) was good, perhaps a tad drawn out, but good none the less.<br /><br />Awesome narration. Was his voice as sexy as Tierney was built up to be?! Perhaps. But such a good voice to spend some hours with on my work commute. <br /><br />I feel at home with this author, she will deliver. It was too long, but delicious and mostly satisfying. I like good names in these types of books and the Lilly/Tierney combo was cool. <br /><br />The creepy voices were great - Mr Witt et. all, those desperate and cunning enough will be sure to receive their cummupence. <br /><br />3.5 stars, rounded nicely to 4.   <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431409223i/14835137.jpg' alt=' photo 5ae020b0bd3ce802ee52bdb758d240be_zpsvpc0wnc6.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>5.11.20<br/>Still reading my SB favorites....and enjoying them all over again! <br/><br/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>5 Chilling Stars!!</b>
</i><br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6218.Sandra_Brown' title='Sandra Brown' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sandra Brown</a> is one of my top "go-to" author's when I'm in the mood for a great mystery suspense that will keep me guessing and on the edge of my seat, and SB manages to add just the right amount of romance to keep the characters connected and the reader enthralled.<br/><br/>In the town of Cleary in North Carolina, four women are missing, and presumed dead. The town has a serial killer (The Blue Ribbon Kill</span>
  <span id="freeText9711150314009796221" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/5ae020b0bd3ce802ee52bdb758d240be_zpsvpc0wnc6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431409223i/14835137.jpg" alt=" photo 5ae020b0bd3ce802ee52bdb758d240be_zpsvpc0wnc6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>5.11.20<br>Still reading my SB favorites....and enjoying them all over again! <br><br><br><br><i>
  <b>5 Chilling Stars!!</b>
</i><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6218.Sandra_Brown" title="Sandra Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Sandra Brown</a> is one of my top "go-to" author's when I'm in the mood for a great mystery suspense that will keep me guessing and on the edge of my seat, and SB manages to add just the right amount of romance to keep the characters connected and the reader enthralled.<br><br>In the town of Cleary in North Carolina, four women are missing, and presumed dead. The town has a serial killer (The Blue Ribbon Killer) on the loose, and as the story unfolds, as usual with a SB novel there are several suspects, and a couple of side stories with many twists and turns.<br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/PicsArt_1463158702936_zps8pbfunlq.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1463162273i/19089139.jpg" alt=" photo PicsArt_1463158702936_zps8pbfunlq.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Lilly Martin, has returned to her ex-husbands hometown of Cleary, NC to close on the sale of their cabin, her ex-husband Dutch is the towns Police Chief who desperately want’s Lilly back. When leaving the cabin during a snow storm her car skids and strikes a man on the side of the road. Ben Tierney, is a man she met the previous summer, and as they wait out the storm together in her cabin they definitely have an attraction to one another, and despite her attraction to Ben she later begins to suspect him as The Blue Ribbon Killer.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>4 women have disappeared from Cleary over the past 2 years ...the greatest danger to Lilly's safety isn't the blizzard outside, but the mysterious man right beside her.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br>I really, really enjoy this one and I found myself engaged in the story, looking for clues and searching for possible suspects. I truly enjoyed all the characters, some were creepy, some sleazy and some downright mysterious.<br> <br>Overall a fast-paced thriller that will keep you guessing with a satisfying ending. I highly recommend to anybody who enjoys a good mystery and a bit of romance, if that’s your preference <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/268275.Chill_Factor" title="Chill Factor by Sandra Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Chill Factor</a> does NOT disappoint!<br><br>* Audio book narrated by the very talented <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/24659.Stephen_Lang" title="Stephen Lang" rel="nofollow noopener">Stephen Lang</a>.<br><br><br><br><br>*Originally read July 2011 (Rated 5 Stars)</span>

<div id="review_1178394789" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1178394789" />
    <a title="Sandra ~ ♥ Cross My Heart ♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17716247-sandra-cross-my-heart"><img alt="Sandra ~ ♥ Cross My Heart ♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415483040p2/17716247.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1178394789?book_show_action=true">Apr 15, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sandra ~ ♥ Cross My Heart ♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sandra ~ ♥ Cross My Heart ♥" href="/user/show/17716247-sandra-cross-my-heart">Sandra ~ ♥ Cross My Heart ♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6382168-chill-factor">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17716247-sandra-cross-my-heart?shelf=romance-suspense">romance-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17716247-sandra-cross-my-heart?shelf=sandra-brown">sandra-brown</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1178394789" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1653791946049611879">Reviewed at: <a href='https://crossmyheartbookreviews.blogspot.com/2017/04/chill-factor-review.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Cross My Heart Writings and Reviews</a><br/><br/>Like most Sandra Brown books, <i>Chill Factor</i> is high on suspense and rich in details with a setting that plays intricately into the story.  The list of possible “who-done-it” candidates is laden with red herrings and the stakes are high.  Like the road that snakes up the mountainside where Lilly Martin finds herself stranded in a cabin during a blizzard, the plot is twisted with s-turns and roadblocks.  If only she had headed down right behind her ex</span>
  <span id="freeText1653791946049611879" style="display:none">Reviewed at: <a href="https://crossmyheartbookreviews.blogspot.com/2017/04/chill-factor-review.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Cross My Heart Writings and Reviews</a><br /><br />Like most Sandra Brown books, <i>Chill Factor</i> is high on suspense and rich in details with a setting that plays intricately into the story.  The list of possible “who-done-it” candidates is laden with red herrings and the stakes are high.  Like the road that snakes up the mountainside where Lilly Martin finds herself stranded in a cabin during a blizzard, the plot is twisted with s-turns and roadblocks.  If only she had headed down right behind her ex-husband, she would have been off the mountain before the storm hit . . . and she wouldn’t be trapped alone in a cabin with a man that she’s extremely attracted to – one that may or may not be a serial killer.  <br /><br />Ben Tierney is a man of mystery.  Very little is known about him other than the fact that he’s an extreme sports writer and attracts women like flies to honey.  Lilly first met him on a kayaking trip the previous summer.  They both felt the jolt of chemistry that passed between them, but Lilly was still married to the very jealous police chief of the small, mountain town at the time.  They parted ways, each wanting but not taking more.  And now, they’ve met again – under much different circumstances.  Five local women are missing, presumed dead.  The town’s people are on edge, tempers are volatile.  The only “stranger” in town is Ben – does that make him the most likely suspect?  Should Lilly trust her heart or follow the evidence? <br /><br /><i>Chill Factor</i> is intense with on-the-edge-of-your seat suspense filling the pages from cover to cover.  The character list is stacked with possible suspects -  damaged, fallible characters with motive, opportunity, and major issues of their own. The rugged, frozen winter setting plays heavily into the storyline as roads are impassable with no one getting up or down the mountain.  Brown is a master at throwing readers off the scent of the real culprit, but I managed to figure this one out early.  But with heart-racing, adrenalin-inducing scenes playing out through the block buster ending, it didn’t lessen my enjoyment.  My only minor issue was the lack of open communication between the hero/heroine with a couple of over-the-top scenes, but still another chilling story by this author.  Another Must Read!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1653791946049611879" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2015995370" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6826679222575243936">Holy crap on a cracker! Ms. Brown can definitely spin a tale. As many books as I have read by her, I am always amazed at her writings. She blew my mind again with this novel. I just knew who the culprit was but I was wrong...over and over again! So many little mysteries inside one big mystery. I loved this book! If you are a true fan of SB, and have never read this one, then grab a copy and enjoy! <br/>.<br/></span>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1608405942" />
    <a title="Ingie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15589375-ingie"><img alt="Ingie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1477339772p2/15589375.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1608405942?book_show_action=true">Apr 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ingie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ingie" href="/user/show/15589375-ingie">Ingie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/6401516-chill-factor">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=romance-m-f-suspense">romance-m-f-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=books-i-read-2016">books-i-read-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=c-amazing-5-stars-2016">c-amazing-5-stars-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1608405942" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11098387034071617559"><i>Review written April 25, 2016</i><br/><br/><b>4 1/2 Stars - Thrilling good romantic (snowy) crime</b><br/><br/>I haven't listened to a <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6218.Sandra_Brown' title='Sandra Brown' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sandra Brown</a> story since August. (Months flies!) Gosh, I have been missing her always so very enjoying romantic crime stories. — This time (my tenth) is it <i>Chill Factor</i>. First published 2005, here the 13:26 hrs audiobook (excellent) narrated by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/24659.Stephen_Lang' title='Stephen Lang' rel='nofollow noopener'>Stephen Lang</a>.<br/><br/><a href='http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Stars/image.jpg2_zps0azoxreu.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430073383i/14677459.jpg' alt=' photo image.jpg2_zps0azoxreu.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>...and I'm breathless</b>.<br/><br/>*******************************************<br/><br/><b>
  <i>«4 women have disappeared from Cleary over the past 2 years. — ...</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText11098387034071617559" style="display:none"><i>Review written April 25, 2016</i><br><br><b>4 1/2 Stars - Thrilling good romantic (snowy) crime</b><br><br>I haven't listened to a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6218.Sandra_Brown" title="Sandra Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Sandra Brown</a> story since August. (Months flies!) Gosh, I have been missing her always so very enjoying romantic crime stories. — This time (my tenth) is it <i>Chill Factor</i>. First published 2005, here the 13:26 hrs audiobook (excellent) narrated by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/24659.Stephen_Lang" title="Stephen Lang" rel="nofollow noopener">Stephen Lang</a>.<br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Stars/image.jpg2_zps0azoxreu.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430073383i/14677459.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg2_zps0azoxreu.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>...and I'm breathless</b>.<br><br>*******************************************<br><br><b>
  <i>«4 women have disappeared from Cleary over the past 2 years. — ...the greatest danger to Lilly's safety isn't the blizzard outside, but the mysterious man right beside her.»</i>
</b><br><br>The successful magazine editor <b>Lilly Martin</b> returns to <i>Cleary, North Carolina</i>, a sleepy mountain town, to close the sale of her mountain cabin and marking the end of her turbulent marriage to the (by now) local chief of police (<i>Dutch Burton</i>). — Soon she is trapped in her cabin with a man (<b>Ben Tierney</b>) believed to be a serial killer.<br><blockquote>
  <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/City%20and%20nature%20etc/winter/image_zpsfp4y7ncn.jpeg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1461598152i/18886513.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsfp4y7ncn.jpeg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote><br><b>Wow! This was nail biting good.</b><br>Exciting, romantic, suspense filled, intriguing and with a large cast with interesting different kind of characters. I didn't have a clue about who the nasty (woman killer) villain was. Kept guessing until the very end. — Also well thoughtout, topics I truly liked, excellent 'whodunnit' crime solving, captivating life stories, and more romantic sweet steam than most SB books. (Yay!!)<br><br><b>On the less good side?</b><br>Maybe were there some (odd) unexplained behaviors from both second and main characters at times. (I didn't really grip why Tierney act like he did always for example.) To be honest was it maybe a (tiny bit) too nicely wrapped in end to be truly believable. Or? But this is fiction, I want sweet and I'm not picky. More 'goodies' than 'baddies'. Add a FANTASTIC narrator. <br><br>All in all: <i>Chill Factor</i> is well spent audiobook hours if you like thrilling romantic suspense / crime in the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6218.Sandra_Brown" title="Sandra Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Sandra Brown</a> genre. I'm just looking forward for more. — Rounded up: a fiver ...'course. <br><br>*******************************************<br><br><b>I LIKE - a crime audiobook is never wrong</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="11098387034071617559" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1066524212" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1066524212" />
    <a title="Karen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6972914-karen"><img alt="Karen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529600203p2/6972914.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1066524212?book_show_action=true">Sep 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karen" href="/user/show/6972914-karen">Karen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6382168-chill-factor">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1066524212" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2014126225290012698"><b>5 STARS</b><br/><span>[image error]</span><a href='http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/0008b800-6fd2-4af3-9c23-26d7f567a54b.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412731681i/11415000._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 0008b800-6fd2-4af3-9c23-26d7f567a54b.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i> "Torrie Lambert vanished as though the ground had opened up and swallowed her. Not a trace of her has been found... except for a blue velvet ribbon."</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>WOW!!!! Loved this one!!! </b> A classic who-done-it psychological thriller with a bit of romance mixed in. This one kept me on the edge of my seat… and the build up had me suspecting EVERYONE. Fabulous writing. <br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><a href='http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/39D5AEAF-CFEE-4AFD-B9D0-E58242833DFA.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412731681i/11415001._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo 39D5AEAF-CFEE-4AFD-B9D0-E58242833DFA.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>The town was <b>Cleary</b>, located in the remote mountains of North Carolina. And it was about to exper</span>
  <span id="freeText2014126225290012698" style="display:none"><b>5 STARS</b><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/0008b800-6fd2-4af3-9c23-26d7f567a54b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412731681i/11415000._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 0008b800-6fd2-4af3-9c23-26d7f567a54b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> "Torrie Lambert vanished as though the ground had opened up and swallowed her. Not a trace of her has been found... except for a blue velvet ribbon."</i>
</b><br><br><b>WOW!!!! Loved this one!!! </b> A classic who-done-it psychological thriller with a bit of romance mixed in. This one kept me on the edge of my seat… and the build up had me suspecting EVERYONE. Fabulous writing. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/39D5AEAF-CFEE-4AFD-B9D0-E58242833DFA.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412731681i/11415001._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 39D5AEAF-CFEE-4AFD-B9D0-E58242833DFA.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The town was <b>Cleary</b>, located in the remote mountains of North Carolina. And it was about to experience the winter storm of the century. The townsfolk were on edge, but not only on account of the weather. 5 women have turned up missing without a trace… well except for the single length of blue ribbon found where each was last seen. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/RCL2671L.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412731681i/11415002._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo RCL2671L.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>A serial killer is suspected.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/ea8f4dcfc8f61987c311b07da202183d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412731681i/11415003._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo ea8f4dcfc8f61987c311b07da202183d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Lilly Martin</b> was saying goodbye to her ex-husband for the last time. They sold their mountain cabin, and met there to clean it out for the closing. It was awkward, and they argued, so despite the on-coming storm they left separately. But the storm was already well under way. Visibility was poor, and traction was worse. So it was no surprise that Lilly was unable to stop for the man on foot, trying to track her down. There was an accident. He was injured. And the only chance they had for survival was trekking back up to the cabin for shelter.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/b8de9636f91bbb53d1199c3cbdf78197.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412731681i/11415004._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo b8de9636f91bbb53d1199c3cbdf78197.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The man was <b>Ben Tierney</b>. A ruggedly handsome man Lilly had met a year ago during a white water rafting trip. He was also a man whom she was deeply attracted to. Tierney was an adventure sports writer who travelled the world writing columns for a popular outdoorsmen magazine. He had been seen from time to time in Cleary, and was quite popular with the ladies of the town. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/captain-reynolds-nathan-fillion.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412731681i/11415005._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo captain-reynolds-nathan-fillion.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Dutch Burton</b> is Lilly’s ex-husband and Cleary’s chief of police. He has been struggling with his career lately as much as his marriage. He has been unable to find a single shred of evidence in the disappearances. <br><br>So because of the pressure of this nagging case, along with the failure of his marriage, he is quickly losing his confidence. He is an alcoholic. He is quick-tempered. And he is still hopelessly in love with his wife. And his composure is slipping.<br><br><b>
  <i> Over time his obsession with failure became a self-fulfilling prophecy.</i>
</b><br><br>Then there is the city councilman/high school football coach, Wes Hamer, who I will kindly refer to as the town asshole and his subservient wife and football star son, Scott. There is the town pharmacist, William Ritt, who gives out town gossip even more than prescriptions; and his old maid sister, and high school teacher, Marilee Ritt.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/1226178543AdP1m1Y.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412731681i/11415006._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 1226178543AdP1m1Y.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There are FBI agents, and simple townsfolk alike, all looking for answers. And they ALL look guilty. But none so much as the man now trapped with Lilly up in her cabin.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/227e0a23c78100495b6e8566e565ec7c-1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412731681i/11415007._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 227e0a23c78100495b6e8566e565ec7c-1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And Lilly… finds herself caught between two realities. Is Ben Tierney, the man of her dreams or the star of her nightmares. Can he really be <i>Blue</i> the suspected serial killer?<br><br><b>
  <i> "Just because you're paranoid doesn't mean everybody still isn't out to get you."</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/27-2746-6LDTD00Z.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380918451i/3247369._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 27-2746-6LDTD00Z.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> "I don't want to sleep.."</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/8aa81c2eba0c0370fb80ae60ae676ca9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412731681i/11415008._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 8aa81c2eba0c0370fb80ae60ae676ca9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And will it be him who takes her life or will it be her own inherent weakness that takes her down in the end?<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/e450380fecb3185aceb1c956d96545c6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412731681i/11415009._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo e450380fecb3185aceb1c956d96545c6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This was a fantastically written story of trust and deception, murder and heroism. How far does someone need to go to prove their innocence… or is it even possible? <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Tags/5a5d872d9851684e5883a50055299b40.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412731681i/11415010.jpg" alt=" photo 5a5d872d9851684e5883a50055299b40.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And will the hysteria of bloodlust building in the town be the downfall of an innocent man?<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/43fe5d8bf0c78f628f417e47aab23b0b-1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412731681i/11415011._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 43fe5d8bf0c78f628f417e47aab23b0b-1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> "I'll be better at it this time, Lilly. I swear to you. I'll love you like you've never been loved."</i>
</b><br><br>Riveting!!! And yes there is romance, but you must be patient. It is hard earned. So far Sandra Brown has proven to be one hell of a great writer. This is the second book of hers that I have read and loved, and it will not be the last! <br><br>Highly recommended!!! <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="2014126225290012698" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_3052841836" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3052841836" />
    <a title="NMmomof4" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4"><img alt="NMmomof4" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515474309p2/24665574.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3052841836?book_show_action=true">Nov 22, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NMmomof4" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NMmomof4" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4">NMmomof4</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=separation-without-other-partners">separation-without-other-partners</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=3-star">3-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=safe">safe</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=scribd">scribd</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=disordered-mc">disordered-mc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=stranded">stranded</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=famous-wealthy-popular">famous-wealthy-popular</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=safe-with-exception">safe-with-exception</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3052841836" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4445353242998383053"><b> 3 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b>I liked the mystery (even though I did figure out who it was pretty early on) and I liked the survival scenes. It was like a marooned romance in the sense that they were stuck together, but I guess I just wanted more romance. There was a lot of side stories going on that I could've done without. I figure it was all to keep the intrigue and mystery going though. One of my issues with romantic suspense is that I often feel like between the romance and suspense there is an </span>
  <span id="freeText4445353242998383053" style="display:none"><b> 3 Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b>I liked the mystery (even though I did figure out who it was pretty early on) and I liked the survival scenes. It was like a marooned romance in the sense that they were stuck together, but I guess I just wanted more romance. There was a lot of side stories going on that I could've done without. I figure it was all to keep the intrigue and mystery going though. One of my issues with romantic suspense is that I often feel like between the romance and suspense there is an imbalance -- and sadly that was the case here. So! If you don't mind these books that lean more heavily on the suspense side with just a dash of romance -- this could be the book for you!<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Lilly and Tierney's story. Lilly gets stuck in the cabin that she just sold after finalizing her divorce. When she tries to get down the mountain in a snow storm, she ends up accidentally hitting Tierney, who was on foot. Tierney and Lilly met the summer before and had connected over a day of kayaking, so they are both shocked to find that they are stranded in a cabin together under some dire conditions in the horrible winter storm. Meanwhile, there has been 5 women kidnapped from the town and Lilly’s police chief ex, as well as the FBI, are on the hunt for answers. There are some suspenseful scenes, some sexy times, the mystery is solved....and Lilly and Tierney get a HFN ending.<br /><br /><b>Point Of View (POV):</b> This alternated between focusing on Lilly and Tierney as well as many other side characters in 3rd person narrative.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. There were a few times where I skimmed because it felt a little too long. I also think this was because of all the side stories going on.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> Kind of. They are in a traumatic situation together, so I understand that it can speed up feelings -- but it felt a little underdeveloped. I'm pretty sure "ILYs" aren't even exchanged or mentioned, other than briefly in the h's inner dialogue.<br /><br /><b>H (Hero) rating:</b> 3 stars. Tierney. I liked him, but I feel as though the author wanted to keep the mystery about him going so we didn't get into too much depth with his character...at least not as much as I'd have liked.<br /><br /><b>h (heroine) rating:</b> 3 stars. Lilly. I also felt like we could've gotten a little deeper into her character, but I didn't dislike her.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Low, no tissues needed<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Both the h and H push away and also pursue the relationship at times. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Alright. They have some tension, chemistry, and scenes -- but not so much it takes away from the story (see below comment).<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes, but a little awkward feeling because I think this is an older book.<br /><br /><b>OW (Other Woman)/OM (Other Man) drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The h's ex husband is the chief of police and he is very jealous of her being with Tierney.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No, but another scene <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[There is a graphic scene with two side characters.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> Yes, but not between mcs <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The h was cheated on repeatedly by her ex and the H's ex fell in love with another man while he was away for work.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are separated at the end, but there was no mention or suggestion of other partners during this time.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Kidnapping/violence/murder (off and on page), loss of a child (off page), both h and H are divorced, and cheating by side characters.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This had an epilogue, but I was bummed out by it tbh. I wanted more of a glimpse into their future! Once the mystery was solved, it felt like a book getting slapped shut. I would call this a HFN ending.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one should be either <u>Safe</u> or <u>Safe with exception</u> for most safety gang readers depending on personal preferences.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating between mcs<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene between side characters (not with mc)<br />- <b> Does</b> have both the h and H pushing away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does </b> have abuse <br />- <b>Does Not </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>
  <a data-text-id="4445353242998383053" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

LOL<br /><br />Apart from freezing feelings it transmits, due to a great descriptions, the book is very, very interesting and until the very end you are not sure who the culprit is!<br /><br />The MCs are secluded in a cabin without light, water or heating. His best friend, who not his friend at all, goads him with lurid suggestions to act even more crazily!<br /><br />I pitied him, even if he is abudding abuser of women. He's clearly mentally instable...<br /><br />I was sitting on the edge while reading this book, because it makes impossible to relax even for a moment!</span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audio CD 9780743544399" href="/book/show/1533888.Chill_Factor">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of psycological thrillers, rather than action</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1133802-fani-loves-angst?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer64475957" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6601482655336545291">I had trouble finishing this and when it's about a suspense story, that means a lot. Plus, the romance part was too weak and unsatisfying IMHO.<br/><br/>Lilly is somehow stranded in an isolated mountain cabin, along with Ben Tierney, a man she's met some months ago and liked. However, women have been disappearing lately in their quiet town and somehow, the more time she spends with him, the more she becomes convinced he's the culprit. Her ex-husband, the town's chief of police, freaks out when he learns t</span>
  <span id="freeText6601482655336545291" style="display:none">I had trouble finishing this and when it's about a suspense story, that means a lot. Plus, the romance part was too weak and unsatisfying IMHO.<br /><br />Lilly is somehow stranded in an isolated mountain cabin, along with Ben Tierney, a man she's met some months ago and liked. However, women have been disappearing lately in their quiet town and somehow, the more time she spends with him, the more she becomes convinced he's the culprit. Her ex-husband, the town's chief of police, freaks out when he learns that she's alone with Tierney and tries to find a way to reach to her, but a recent ice-storm has closed all roads to the cabin.<br />Meanwhile, we meet some other town citizens and gain insight in their own stories. Many of them seem to be hiding secrets from each other. Could one of them have anything to do with the disappearing women after all?<br /><br />This is a book with too much suspense but little action. It was more character rather than action driven, and after a while it became too slow and tiring for me. Besides, I didn't care much for the heroine and especially not the hero. I was far more interested in some of the secondary characters and their secrets than who the villain is. At least, the pace and action picked up considerably near the end. <br /><br /></span>

Definitely cheated on her a bunch.  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/>Love triangle: <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ No  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/>Sex with om/ow: <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ No  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/>Intimate pasts: <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ I really don't know but based on inner thoughts and conversations I'll have to guess my take on this.   <span id="freeText16121369519526137693" style="display:none">Overall rating: 4.75 stars!<br /><br />Triggers:<br />Cheating: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Not between the hero and heroine, but of course, the heroine's ex husband is a piece of work. Definitely cheated on her a bunch.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />Love triangle: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ No  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />Sex with om/ow: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ No  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />Intimate pasts: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I really don't know but based on inner thoughts and conversations I'll have to guess my take on this. For the heroine, she wasn't a virgin, but was married and it's really unclear how long it's been for her. I know it's been several months for sure since she has been separated from her husband, but before that? I don't know. She mentions that it's been 4 years, but that could be including the not so great sex her and her husband had due to their issues and their grief. For the hero, I would say it's been awhile for him. There isn't confirmed, BUT when the FBI are looking into him and questioning people, no one has ever seen him with a woman in the last two years. The only thoughts about ow were when the local town's men (who were jealous of him) would say that women flocked to him, meaning that they liked his rugged looks and such. But it was more so that they swooned over him, not that they ever saw him with ow. The hero and heroine met several months ago prior to the heroine's divorce and shared a moment. No sexual contact or anything like that, but a connection. That same day, this group of college girls were apparently flirting with him and when the heroine asks him if he went to their house since she turned him down, he doesn't respond. I'm not sure why, however, once I found out more about him and what he was going through and what he was doing at the time, I would find it hard to believe if he did go with them. I'm not saying he was a monk during this time, but knowing what I found out about him and what he was going through, I wouldn't be surprised if he wasn't with anyone in a few years. I won't ruin the story/plot and reveal what I learned about him. Going into Sandra Brown's books blind is the best way to go.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />Push/pull: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The hero is very interested in the heroine from their very first meeting. I'd say all the pushing away comes from the heroine.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />OW/OM drama: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I would say no. The heroine's ex comes into play but not in the way you think. She doesn't have feelings for him like that anymore, but she does care for him as a person and the devastating events that they shared. There are no OW that show up for the hero at all.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />HEA: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes and it actually was a very sweet one. Of course, I wanted more, but I know how Sandra Brown doesn't always give us our nice in the future HEA LOL  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I really enjoyed this book. I will have to say once again that her books are more suspense than romance, but in this particular book, there was an underlying romance the entire time. You know the hero has intense feelings for the heroine. There was one love scene and more implied towards the end of the book, so not very steamy at all. <br /><br />This book definitely had many twists and turns and kept you guessing till the very end. I don't really give too much information on her plot lines because they are meant to be revealed the way the author writes them. So I'm sorry if my spoilers even sounds vague, but that's the best way to go into this book LOL. </span>

<div id="review_3140736244" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3140736244" />
    <a title="Nadene  (Totally Addicted to Reading)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9324688-nadene-totally-addicted-to-reading"><img alt="Nadene  (Totally Addicted to Reading)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605785947p2/9324688.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3140736244?book_show_action=true">Jan 16, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nadene  (Totally Addicted to Reading)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nadene  (Totally Addicted to Reading)" href="/user/show/9324688-nadene-totally-addicted-to-reading">Nadene  (Totally Addicted to Reading)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6382168-chill-factor">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3140736244" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10778083769653568723">I have a few Sandra Brown books on my shelves, and I hope to read them all for 2020. The next of her books on my list was Chill Factor. I was ecstatic when I discovered it was also in Kindle Unlimited so I went with reading the e-book version which made things simpler, when I needed to read during my lunchtime at work.<br/><br/>Chill Factor proved to be an interesting read. The story takes place in the small town of Cleary, where nothing is secret. Gossip, blackmail and the illegal dispensing of drugs is </span>
  <span id="freeText10778083769653568723" style="display:none">I have a few Sandra Brown books on my shelves, and I hope to read them all for 2020. The next of her books on my list was Chill Factor. I was ecstatic when I discovered it was also in Kindle Unlimited so I went with reading the e-book version which made things simpler, when I needed to read during my lunchtime at work.<br /><br />Chill Factor proved to be an interesting read. The story takes place in the small town of Cleary, where nothing is secret. Gossip, blackmail and the illegal dispensing of drugs is rampant in this little town and it would appear that the chief of police had no control over the illicit activities. He could not even solve the case of the five women who had gone missing in the last two years, all because he got caught up in his own personal issues.<br /><br />I thought the mystery was well done. It had me guessing from the start the identity of the person responsible for the missing women and wondering what was their motive. What made this interesting and had me thinking was the fact that the five women who had gone missing had nothing common except for their kidnapper/killer. There were so many things happening and it was hard figuring out who could be trusted. There were so many suspects, which also included the male protagonist Ben Tierney. Yep, this added to intrigue. I didn’t like how the FBI handled the situation to begin with, but they redeemed themselves.<br /><br />The characters proved an interesting bunch. We have Lilly, who finds herself stranded in her cabin with a man she is attracted to, but who may be a serial killer. Ben (Tierney), who proved difficult to read and who has the hots or Lilly. Dutch, the chief of police and Lilly’s ex-husband who was manipulative, selfish, and a serial cheater. Wes, the chief’s best friend a womanizer who had an ego the size of the Pacific Ocean. Then there was Scott, who was heading down a road of self-destruction, which was inevitable with a father like Wes. Then we have William, the town’s pharmacist and his spinster sister Marilee. These two came with their own brand of issues stemming from losing their parents at an early age and a host of other problems.<br /><br />The story focused on the happenings in the town and the search for the villain, therefore the romance took a back seat. One could not deny the chemistry between Ben and Lilly. They were not strangers as they had met a year ago, but only for a short time. So, their being trapped in her cabin was a reunion of sorts.<br /><br />Conclusion/Recommendation<br />Fans of romantic suspense would love Chill Factor. It’s entertaining, riveting and filled with several twists.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10778083769653568723" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer18260942224165447736">Listened to this book on the drive to and from SC at Thanksgiving. It was a way to fill up the long and empty miles, but as a piece of "literachoor" - it was an enormous piece of feculent nonsense.<br/><br/>Where to start? How about the part where Lily, the heroine, convinced she is snowed in with a serial kidnapper/murderer, has hot monkey sex with him, despite the whole HE'S A FREAKIN' MURDERER thing.<br/><br/>Or how about the fact that the hot, monkey sex happens between a woman who is weak from a nearly-fatal a</span>
  <span id="freeText18260942224165447736" style="display:none">Listened to this book on the drive to and from SC at Thanksgiving. It was a way to fill up the long and empty miles, but as a piece of "literachoor" - it was an enormous piece of feculent nonsense.<br /><br />Where to start? How about the part where Lily, the heroine, convinced she is snowed in with a serial kidnapper/murderer, has hot monkey sex with him, despite the whole HE'S A FREAKIN' MURDERER thing.<br /><br />Or how about the fact that the hot, monkey sex happens between a woman who is weak from a nearly-fatal asthma attack and a man who has:<br />a concussion<br />bruises all over his body from being HIT BY A CAR<br />an open head wound<br />a sprained ankle.<br />Plus, the HMS takes place in a freezing cold cabin where the two people are marooned. So cold that normal people would just be curled up INSIDE the fireplace, not getting naked in front of it. Jeez. I realize it's fiction, but couldn't there be some sense of 'this could really happen?'<br /><br />The side story about the high school athlete, steroids,<br />the worst father in the world, and his dishrag of a wife was just distasteful.<br /><br />Won't be reading / listening to any more Sandra Brown, that's for sure.<br /><br /></span>

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2207539-steen?shelf=2009-books">2009-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2207539-steen?shelf=hated">hated</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer61060772&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer61060772" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15931567880757594907">I hated this book. By the time I realized it wasn't going to get better I was pretty well done it so I continued. I didn't know it was possible to write a book where the reader hates every single character. There wasn't one that I cared for at all. Maybe there could have been but the story wasn't really about them so they were insignificant. I'm sorry the LAST thing I would be doing if I am stuck in a blizzard, in a cabin with no heat/hydro etc would be to worry about taking a sponge bath and pr</span>
  <span id="freeText15931567880757594907" style="display:none">I hated this book. By the time I realized it wasn't going to get better I was pretty well done it so I continued. I didn't know it was possible to write a book where the reader hates every single character. There wasn't one that I cared for at all. Maybe there could have been but the story wasn't really about them so they were insignificant. I'm sorry the LAST thing I would be doing if I am stuck in a blizzard, in a cabin with no heat/hydro etc would be to worry about taking a sponge bath and proceeding to do that by taking off all your clothes. HELLO its freezing outside - I don't care if they had a fire going its still cold. ~rolls eyes. There are more situations like that that just seemed so unbelieveable, I know its fiction but still. I rolled my eyes a lot of the time. I also don't see what she saw in Tiereny - his questions were down right rude and the whole 'none of your business' comes into mind. Especially since she really didnt know him. Whatever I could go on but whats the point. It just wasn't to my liking.<br /><br />All though I do have to give Sandra Brown the fact that it did keep my interest enough to finish it. I didn't just throw it down. Although I found it to be much to long and it dragged on in spots. I also really didn't see that twist coming at the end but even then I really didnt care enough about any of them to care. Oh well onto other books...</span>
